 loadQueue[i]();
 delete loadQueue;
 };

  :host {
    --mr-edit-field-padding: 0.125em 4px;
    --mr-edit-field-width: 90%;

    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);

    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
    background: var(--chops-white);
    border-radius: 6px;
    --chops-button-padding: 0.25em 8px;
    margin: 0;
    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
    font-weight: normal;
    line-height: 1;
    padding: 0.25em 0;
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    margin: 0;
    margin-top: 0.25em;
    border-bottom: var(--chops-normal-border);
  }
  .medium-heading chops-button {
    line-height: 1.6;
  }
  .input-grid {
    padding: 0.5em 0;
    display: grid;
    max-width: 100%;
    grid-gap: var(--mr-input-grid-gap);
    grid-template-columns: minmax(120px, max-content) 1fr;
    align-items: flex-start;
  }
  .input-grid label {
    font-weight: bold;
    text-align: right;
    word-wrap: break-word;
  }
  @media (max-width: 600px) {
    .input-grid label {
      margin-top: var(--mr-input-grid-gap);
      text-align: left;
    }
    .input-grid {
      grid-gap: var(--mr-input-grid-gap);
      grid-template-columns: 100%;
    }
  }

        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

          z-index: 200;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Changing the URL using `history.replaceState` to 10M+ characters causes a spoofing bug in various security UIs.



<span class="line"><!---->Changing the URL using `history.replaceState` to 10M+ characters causes a spoofing bug in various security UIs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 94.0.4606.71 + all channels



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 94.0.4606.71 + all channels<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Tested on Windows 10, Mac OS, Android 11



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Tested on Windows 10, Mac OS, Android 11<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





# Classic Tab



<span class="line"><!----># Classic Tab<!----></span>



<br>





1. Open 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Open <!----></span>





https://example.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://example.com"><!---->https://example.com<!----></a>



<br>





2. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`



<span class="line"><!---->2. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`<!----></span>



<br>





3. URL is `about:blank#blocked`



<span class="line"><!---->3. URL is `about:blank#blocked`<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





# Payment Dialog



<span class="line"><!----># Payment Dialog<!----></span>



<br>





1. Go to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Go to <!----></span>





https://liquangumax.github.io/apps/max-nonbasiccard/



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://liquangumax.github.io/apps/max-nonbasiccard/"><!---->https://liquangumax.github.io/apps/max-nonbasiccard/<!----></a>





 and Install



<span class="line"><!----> and Install<!----></span>



<br>





2. Go to 



<span class="line"><!---->2. Go to <!----></span>





https://maxlgu.github.io/pr/max-nonbasiccard/



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://maxlgu.github.io/pr/max-nonbasiccard/"><!---->https://maxlgu.github.io/pr/max-nonbasiccard/<!----></a>





 and click Buy



<span class="line"><!----> and click Buy<!----></span>



<br>





3. Navigate the payment dialog to 



<span class="line"><!---->3. Navigate the payment dialog to <!----></span>





https://example.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://example.com"><!---->https://example.com<!----></a>



<br>





4. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`



<span class="line"><!---->4. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`<!----></span>



<br>





5. URL is not displayed



<span class="line"><!---->5. URL is not displayed<!----></span>



<br>





6. (Optionally) change the title: `document.title='https:\u200e//google.com'`



<span class="line"><!---->6. (Optionally) change the title: `document.title='https:\u200e//google.com'`<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





# Screen Share Dialog



<span class="line"><!----># Screen Share Dialog<!----></span>



<br>





1. Open 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Open <!----></span>





https://example.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://example.com"><!---->https://example.com<!----></a>



<br>





2. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`



<span class="line"><!---->2. Eval: `history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + '?' + 'x'.repeat(10000000));`<!----></span>



<br>





3. Eval: `navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia()`



<span class="line"><!---->3. Eval: `navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia()`<!----></span>



<br>





4. Page origin is not displayed in the dialog.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Page origin is not displayed in the dialog.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





Attached are screenshots of the bug in various UIs.



<span class="line"><!---->Attached are screenshots of the bug in various UIs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->CREDIT INFORMATION<!----></b>

Thanks for the report.  As 



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for the report.  As <!----></span>





comment 2



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c2"><!---->comment 2<!----></a>





 notes, this is more about causing a missing URL or a confusing "about:blank#blocked" URL to show in dialogs, rather than showing an attacker-controlled URL, but in some of the cases it still appears to be an issue in practice.



<span class="line"><!----> notes, this is more about causing a missing URL or a confusing "about:blank#blocked" URL to show in dialogs, rather than showing an attacker-controlled URL, but in some of the cases it still appears to be an issue in practice.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For this specific approach, maybe there's a way to enforce an identical length limit in the renderer process to avoid failing the FilterURL check, but I'm not sure if that would rule out all the ways FilterURL might rewrite it to about:blank#blocked.



<span class="line"><!---->For this specific approach, maybe there's a way to enforce an identical length limit in the renderer process to avoid failing the FilterURL check, but I'm not sure if that would rule out all the ways FilterURL might rewrite it to about:blank#blocked.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





More generally, dialogs probably need to be more robust to about:blank-like URLs (as discussed in 



<span class="line"><!---->More generally, dialogs probably need to be more robust to about:blank-like URLs (as discussed in <!----></span>





issue 1241497



<span class="line"><!---->issue 1241497<!----></span>





 and



<span class="line"><!----> and<!----></span>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





issue 1228702



<span class="line"><!---->issue 1228702<!----></span>





).



<span class="line"><!---->).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I don't think tab-url-spoof.png and window-url-spoof.png are significant concerns (since the attacker can't put a victim's URL in the address bar), but some of the other screenshots are concerning:



<span class="line"><!---->I don't think tab-url-spoof.png and window-url-spoof.png are significant concerns (since the attacker can't put a victim's URL in the address bar), but some of the other screenshots are concerning:<!----></span>



<br>





* payment-dialog-custom-title-spoof.png shows no URL, allowing the title to look like a URL.  This is a problem.



<span class="line"><!---->* payment-dialog-custom-title-spoof.png shows no URL, allowing the title to look like a URL.  This is a problem.<!----></span>



<br>





* permission-access-denied-spoof.png is confusing if not necessarily dangerous?



<span class="line"><!---->* permission-access-denied-spoof.png is confusing if not necessarily dangerous?<!----></span>



<br>





* pwa-custom-title-spoof.png at least shows about:blank#blocked, but also allows an attacker-controlled title.  Might be a problem.



<span class="line"><!---->* pwa-custom-title-spoof.png at least shows about:blank#blocked, but also allows an attacker-controlled title.  Might be a problem.<!----></span>



<br>





* The screen-share images also show a missing and confusing URL.



<span class="line"><!---->* The screen-share images also show a missing and confusing URL.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Origin might be a better thing to display in all these cases?  avi@ / meacer@: Do you have thoughts on how to address this more generally?



<span class="line"><!---->Origin might be a better thing to display in all these cases?  avi@ / meacer@: Do you have thoughts on how to address this more generally?<!----></span>

For the screen sharing dialog, the string comes from DisplayMediaAccessHandler::ProcessQueuedAccessRequest() which tries to do the right thing but hits an antipattern.



<span class="line"><!---->For the screen sharing dialog, the string comes from DisplayMediaAccessHandler::ProcessQueuedAccessRequest() which tries to do the right thing but hits an antipattern.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





They could have done:



<span class="line"><!---->They could have done:<!----></span>



<br>





   picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatUrlForSecurityDisplay(



<span class="line"><!---->   picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatUrlForSecurityDisplay(<!----></span>



<br>





       web_contents->GetLastCommittedURL(),



<span class="line"><!---->       web_contents-&gt;GetLastCommittedURL(),<!----></span>



<br>





       url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);



<span class="line"><!---->       url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





which would say “about:blank#blocked wants to share the contents of your screen”.



<span class="line"><!---->which would say “about:blank#blocked wants to share the contents of your screen”.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





They could have done:



<span class="line"><!---->They could have done:<!----></span>



<br>





   picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay(



<span class="line"><!---->   picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay(<!----></span>



<br>





       web_contents->GetMainFrame()->GetLastCommittedOrigin(),



<span class="line"><!---->       web_contents-&gt;GetMainFrame()-&gt;GetLastCommittedOrigin(),<!----></span>



<br>





       url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);



<span class="line"><!---->       url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





which would correctly say 



<span class="line"><!---->which would correctly say <!----></span>





“



<span class="line"><!---->“<!----></span>





example.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://example.com"><!---->example.com<!----></a>





 wants to share the contents of your screen”.



<span class="line"><!----> wants to share the contents of your screen”.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





But they did:



<span class="line"><!---->But they did:<!----></span>



<br>





  picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay(



<span class="line"><!---->  picker_params.app_name = url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay(<!----></span>



<br>





      url::Origin::Create(web_contents->GetLastCommittedURL()),



<span class="line"><!---->      url::Origin::Create(web_contents-&gt;GetLastCommittedURL()),<!----></span>



<br>





      url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);



<span class="line"><!---->      url_formatter::SchemeDisplay::OMIT_CRYPTOGRAPHIC);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





and url::Origin::Create() creates a null origin, which url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay turns into an empty string.



<span class="line"><!---->and url::Origin::Create() creates a null origin, which url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay turns into an empty string.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Issues here:



<span class="line"><!---->Issues here:<!----></span>



<br>





1. The fact that “about:blank#blocked” turns into a null Origin isn’t great.



<span class="line"><!---->1. The fact that “about:blank#blocked” turns into a null Origin isn’t great.<!----></span>



<br>





2. `FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay` should probably hard-CHECK if a null Origin is passed to it.



<span class="line"><!---->2. `FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay` should probably hard-CHECK if a null Origin is passed to it.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Can we do anything about the antipattern of `url::Origin::Create(web_contents->GetLastCommittedURL())`?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Can we do anything about the antipattern of `url::Origin::Create(web_contents-&gt;GetLastCommittedURL())`?<!----></span>

Specifically, the antipattern `url::Origin::Create(web_contents->GetLastCommittedURL())` allows a page to launder its origin into an opaque origin unrelated to its URL.



<span class="line"><!---->Specifically, the antipattern `url::Origin::Create(web_contents-&gt;GetLastCommittedURL())` allows a page to launder its origin into an opaque origin unrelated to its URL.<!----></span>

Media sharing is fixed. Payments on desktop is fixed, but payments on Android requires infrastructure for Java Origin that doesn’t yet exist and is being discussed. PWAs show URLs in CustomTabBarView::UpdateContents() but it shares a lot of infrastructure with the omnibox so it’s not clear to me how to fix it.



<span class="line"><!---->Media sharing is fixed. Payments on desktop is fixed, but payments on Android requires infrastructure for Java Origin that doesn’t yet exist and is being discussed. PWAs show URLs in CustomTabBarView::UpdateContents() but it shares a lot of infrastructure with the omnibox so it’s not clear to me how to fix it.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What else is there to do? Do we want to do a more thorough retrofit of Origin?



<span class="line"><!---->What else is there to do? Do we want to do a more thorough retrofit of Origin?<!----></span>

What else can be done here?



<span class="line"><!---->What else can be done here?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The immediate issue of missing origins in the dialogs is fixed (at least on desktop). There remain underlying issues: That GURL.GetOrigin returns a GURL (though it’s been renamed), that Origin::Create is still problematic, that the Origin infrastructure on Android is underbuilt and some of the fixes on desktop cannot be made on Android until that happens.



<span class="line"><!---->The immediate issue of missing origins in the dialogs is fixed (at least on desktop). There remain underlying issues: That GURL.GetOrigin returns a GURL (though it’s been renamed), that Origin::Create is still problematic, that the Origin infrastructure on Android is underbuilt and some of the fixes on desktop cannot be made on Android until that happens.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Is this something that we need to assemble a task force to handle, or do we call this bug done?



<span class="line"><!---->Is this something that we need to assemble a task force to handle, or do we call this bug done?<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

           * there's spacing. */

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {

          text-decoration: underline;

          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;

          width: 1px;
